posted:Posted May 4, 2024
msg:The room was very good and was upgraded. The hotel is a garden-style resort hotel with villas scattered along the lake. It has been raining for several days. I didn't walk around the hotel properly and didn't notice if there was a place suitable for walking. The road inside the hotel is relatively narrow and battery cars pass through from time to time. It is really not suitable for walking. Go to the lobby or swimming pool, call and there will be a battery car to deliver immediately. The service is really good. The breakfast is OK, but it feels that the place is not very big. It is difficult to find a seat during peak hours or the clean seats are not cleared in time. The lobby manager Zheng Danni is warm and thoughtful. I added WeChat on the first day and said that I could tell her if I had any requirements. I also enthusiastically sent children's toys and snack packs. Such a lobby manager really enhances the good image of Saint-Germain! The room service Deng Meizhi cleaned the house very cleanly and came to deliver water late at night. Thank you very much! The hotel is 15 kilometers away from Orange Island and 38 minutes by car. It is a little far from the city, but it wins in beautiful environment and good service, which is suitable for vacation. Swimming and fitness are good, there are trees everywhere, but there is no green space or garden for walking, unlike the resort hotel of Shangri-La in Sanya. However, this is in the city after all, and cannot be compared with the seaside hotel. Overall, the price-performance ratio of Saint-Germain is still very high. The five-star hotels in the city center are much more expensive than here, but the comfort is definitely not as good as here. Here you will be woken up by the birds every day, and it really feels like a vacation. It is best to drive by yourself. The car is parked on the roadside or in the underground garage under the villa, which is very convenient! Next door is Hunan Satellite TV and Hunan Radio and Television Center. It is said that many celebrities who participated in Hunan TV programs live here, but I haven't met them yet! Highly recommended, I will stay here next time I come to Changsha!

早餐：

性價比：

3、坐上電瓶車（車一直在循環開，很快，基本不用等很久），開車的小哥特別好，行李是幫忙拎上房間的

現在很少看到服務這麼不拉挎的酒店了，一路上服務人員都很熱情周到，國際五星通常有種疏遠的客氣，這裏我真的感受到了服務，五星好評，望保持

另外看芒果的演唱會這裏太方便了，出芒果廳一轉電瓶車已經在邊上候着了。

msg:地理位置：對於一個追星目的的人來説這家酒店的位置可謂是最佳沒有之一，離市中心打車大概二十幾分鍾，離機場三十分鐘。位置比較偏，但隔壁就是芒果tv，這才是最重要的。
硬件設施：大堂到房間（獨棟）需要酒店的小車車，但一個電話就可以叫到，不成問題。房間裏的設施比較陳舊，空調很不給力，淋浴間下水不暢水會外溢，其他的還可以接受。
酒店服務：唯一能cover掉硬件不足的就是服務，客房服務員小林小吳都非常負責，幾乎隨叫隨到的程度，非常滿意。禮賓部小王更是要重點表揚，某天趕着去隔壁芒果，小王很精準判斷了我的需求，並且很貼心的把我送到了最近的一個地點，還給了温馨提示，瞬間好感度拉滿。酒店領導請看看我的真實評價吧，給小王加雞腿啊！
如果酒店能把我提到的硬件不足解決，下一次如果目的一樣的話還是會願意住這裏的。

msg:除了極差的酒店我會評價，應該是第一次寫酒店評價。
首先，五星好評給予酒店工作人員唐賽陽唐姐，因為天氣突然轉涼在世界之窗園區很冷，聯繫酒店有沒有跑腿，結果唐姐直接給一家大小外套全送到景區安檢處，這是這一趟出行暖1；其次是離店，唐姐也特地來送行，暖2；住店的每天都有溝通住店體驗感，暖3。
其次，評價酒店位置，是帶小孩子旅遊絕佳的酒店，毗鄰世界之窗、海底世界、芒果TV，出園區保安亭聯繫酒店有車接送，全程輕鬆帶娃。
這是一趟輕鬆且滿意的出行，感謝唐姐的體貼服務，為這次出行增添了光環，茫茫人海有緣再見，祝您及家人國慶假期快樂。
